                    WHERE 0 = [Extent1].[IsDeleted] ) AS [Filter1]
                LEFT OUTER JOIN [dbo].[T_IdNames] AS [Extent8] ON [Filter1].[TypeId] = [Extent8].[Id]

            ORDER BY [Project1].[CreateDateTime] DESC
            OFFSET 0 ROWS FETCH NEXT 10 ROWS ONLY  ) AS [Limit1]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN [dbo].[T_HousePics] AS [Extent9] ON [Limit1].[Id] = [Extent9].[HouseId]
    )  AS [Project2]
    ORDER BY [Project2].[CreateDateTime] DESC, [Project2].[Id1] ASC, [Project2].[Id2] ASC, [Project2].[Id] ASC, [Project2].[Id3] ASC, [Project2].[Id4] ASC, [Project2].[Id5] ASC, [Project2].[Id6] ASC, [Project2].[Id7] ASC, [Project2].[C1] ASC
